Presentation Script (When Delivering This Slide):
Opening:
"Before we wrap up, I want to address the enterprise buying criteriaâ€”because I know these matter for organizations of your scale."

Security:
"[Point to Security section] First, security and compliance. We're SOC 2 Type II certified. We're GDPR, HIPAA, and CCPA compliant. We do quarterly penetration testing by third parties. And we support all the security features you'd expectâ€”end-to-end encryption, zero-trust architecture, SSO integration, complete audit trails.

Your data stays in your network, in your VPC, under your control. We never see your actual dataâ€”we just process it according to your policies."

Scale:
"[Point to Scale section] Second, scale. We're proven at petabyte scale, processing billions of events per day. We have a 99.9% uptime SLA with zero data loss guarantees. We support multi-cloud, on-premises, hybrid, and edge deployments. And we auto-scale to handle your peak loads plus 50% headroom."

Support:
"[Point to Support section] Third, support. Every Enterprise customer gets a named Technical Account Managerâ€”24/7/365. You get a 1-hour response SLA for critical issues. You have direct access to our engineering team. You get quarterly business reviews, architecture reviews, and input into our product roadmap.

This isn't throw-it-over-the-wall software. We're your partner in success."

Partnerships:
"[Point to Partnerships section] Fourth, partnerships. We're an AWS Technology Partner, Microsoft Partner, and Google Cloud Partner. We're a Snowflake Technology Partner and Databricks Technology Partner. We work closely with the platforms you already use to make them better, not replace them."

Financial Stability:
"[Point to Financial section] And finally, financial stability. We're backed by General Catalyst and other tier-one investors. We've raised [amount] in funding with 3+ years of runway. We're growing 200% year-over-year with 95% customer retention. We're not going anywhere."

Closing:
"The bottom line: Expanso is enterprise-ready from day one. We have the security, the scale, the support, the partnerships, and the financial backing to be your long-term data platform partner."

Objection Handling Built Into This Slide:
Objection 1: "Are you secure enough for our requirements?"
Answer Built In: SOC 2 Type II, GDPR/HIPAA/CCPA, quarterly pen testing

Objection 2: "Can you handle our scale?"
Answer Built In: Petabyte-scale, billions of events/day, 99.9% SLA

Objection 3: "What if we need help at 2 AM?"
Answer Built In: 24x7x365 support, 1-hour P1 response SLA, named TAM

Objection 4: "Will this integrate with our existing tools?"
Answer Built In: 50+ connectors, partnerships with major platforms

Objection 5: "What if you go out of business?"
Answer Built In: Well-funded, 200% growth, 95% retention, tier-one investors

When to Use This Slide:
Use During Presentation If:
Selling to Fortune 500 or large enterprise
Security/compliance is a known concern
CIO, CISO, or CFO in the room
Procurement or legal team involved
Multi-year contract discussion
Use as Backup If:
Selling to mid-market (may not need all details)
Technical audience (may care more about features)
Time-constrained presentation
Early-stage discussion
Always Have Ready For:
Security questionnaires
Vendor risk assessments
Procurement due diligence
Legal contract negotiations
Executive approval processes

Company overview (one-pager)
Investor information
Growth metrics (if public)
Customer references
Analyst reports (if available)

â”‚  Q: What counts as a "node"?                                â”‚
â”‚  A: A node is any server, VM, or edge location where       â”‚
â”‚     Expanso agents run. Typically: application servers,     â”‚
â”‚     data sources, or edge gateways.                         â”‚
â”‚                                                             â”‚
â”‚  Q: Do you charge per GB of data processed?                â”‚
â”‚  A: No. Our per-node pricing includes unlimited data       â”‚
â”‚     volume. Process terabytes or petabytesâ€”same price.      â”‚
â”‚                                                             â”‚
â”‚  Q: What if our node count fluctuates?                     â”‚
â”‚  A: We true-up annually based on average node count.       â”‚
â”‚     Add nodes anytime (prorated). No penalties for          â”‚
â”‚     reducing at renewal.                                    â”‚
â”‚                                                             â”‚
â”‚  Q: Are there any hidden fees?                             â”‚
â”‚  A: No. Pricing includes all features, support,            â”‚
â”‚     implementation, training, and updates. No egress,       â”‚
â”‚     storage, or compute charges.                            â”‚
â”‚                                                             â”‚
â”‚  Q: Can we start small and expand?                         â”‚

â”‚     apply automatically as you grow.                        â”‚
â”‚                                                             â”‚

Policy Framework:


â”Œâ”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”
â”‚  POLICY ENGINE ARCHITECTURE:                                â”‚
â”‚                                                             â”‚
â”‚  POLICY TYPES:                                              â”‚
â”‚                                                             â”‚
â”‚  ğŸ” FILTERING POLICIES:                                      â”‚
â”‚  â€¢ Drop: Remove unwanted data (e.g., DEBUG logs)           â”‚
â”‚  â€¢ Sample: Keep percentage of data (e.g., 10% of metrics)  â”‚
â”‚  â€¢ Deduplicate: Remove duplicate events                    â”‚
â”‚  â€¢ Conditional: Filter based on field values               â”‚
â”‚                                                             â”‚
â”‚  Example Policy (YAML):                                     â”‚
â”‚  ```yaml                                                    â”‚
â”‚  name: drop-debug-logs                                      â”‚
â”‚  type: filter                                               â”‚
â”‚  condition: log_level == "DEBUG"                            â”‚
â”‚  action: drop                                               â”‚
â”‚  ```                                                        â”‚
â”‚                                                             â”‚
â”‚  âš¡ TRANSFORMATION POLICIES:                                 â”‚
â”‚  â€¢ Parse: Extract structured data from unstructured        â”‚
â”‚  â€¢ Enrich: Add metadata or lookup data                     â”‚
â”‚  â€¢ Aggregate: Summarize data (e.g., metrics rollup)        â”‚
â”‚  â€¢ Format: Convert between formats (JSON, Parquet, etc.)   â”‚
â”‚                                                             â”‚
â”‚  Example Policy (YAML):                                     â”‚
â”‚  ```yaml                                                    â”‚
â”‚  name: enrich-with-geo                                      â”‚
â”‚  type: transform                                            â”‚
â”‚  source_field: ip_address                                   â”‚
â”‚  lookup: geoip_database                                     â”‚
â”‚  target_fields: [country, city, lat, lon]                  â”‚
â”‚  ```                                                        â”‚
â”‚                                                             â”‚
â”‚  ğŸ”’ GOVERNANCE POLICIES:                                     â”‚
â”‚  â€¢ Detect: Identify PII/PHI using ML models                â”‚
â”‚  â€¢ Mask: Redact or tokenize sensitive data                 â”‚
â”‚  â€¢ Classify: Tag data with sensitivity levels              â”‚
â”‚  â€¢ Audit: Log all data access and transformations          â”‚
â”‚                                                             â”‚
â”‚  Example Policy (YAML):                                     â”‚
â”‚  ```yaml                                                    â”‚
â”‚  name: mask-credit-cards                                    â”‚
â”‚  type: governance                                           â”‚
â”‚  detect: credit_card_number                                 â”‚
â”‚  action: mask                                               â”‚
â”‚  method: last_four_digits                                   â”‚
â”‚  ```                                                        â”‚
â”‚                                                             â”‚
â”‚  ğŸ¯ ROUTING POLICIES:                                        â”‚
â”‚  â€¢ Route: Send data to specific destinations               â”‚
â”‚  â€¢ Fanout: Send to multiple destinations                   â”‚
â”‚  â€¢ Conditional: Route based on data content                â”‚
â”‚  â€¢ Priority: High-value to expensive, low-value to cheap   â”‚
â”‚                                                             â”‚
â”‚  Example Policy (YAML):                                     â”‚
â”‚  ```yaml                                                    â”‚
â”‚  name: intelligent-routing                                  â”‚
â”‚  type: route                                                â”‚
â”‚  rules:                                                     â”‚
â”‚    - condition: priority == "high"                          â”‚
â”‚      destination: snowflake                                 â”‚
â”‚    - condition: priority == "low"                           â”‚
â”‚      destination: s3_archive                                â”‚
â”‚  ```                                                        â”‚
â”‚                                                             â”‚
â””â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”˜
Security Architecture:


â”Œâ”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”
â”‚  SECURITY BY DESIGN:                                        â”‚
â”‚                                                             â”‚
â”‚  ğŸ” DATA SECURITY:                                           â”‚
â”‚  â€¢ Encryption in transit: TLS 1.3 (mTLS for agent comms)   â”‚
â”‚  â€¢ Encryption at rest: AES-256                              â”‚
â”‚  â€¢ Zero-knowledge architecture (we never see your data)     â”‚
â”‚  â€¢ Data processed in your VPC/network                       â”‚
â”‚  â€¢ No data stored in Expanso infrastructure                 â”‚
â”‚                                                             â”‚
â”‚  ğŸ›¡ï¸  NETWORK SECURITY:                                       â”‚
â”‚  â€¢ Private VPC deployment                                   â”‚

â”‚  â€¢ Network segmentation                                     â”‚
â”‚  â€¢ Firewall-friendly (outbound only)                        â”‚
â”‚                                                             â”‚
â”‚  ğŸ”‘ ACCESS CONTROL:                                          â”‚

â”‚  â€¢ Multi-factor authentication (MFA)                        â”‚
â”‚  â€¢ API key management with rotation                         â”‚
â”‚  â€¢ Service account isolation                                â”‚
â”‚                                                             â”‚
â”‚  ğŸ“ AUDIT & COMPLIANCE:                                      â”‚

â”‚  HIGH AVAILABILITY ARCHITECTURE:                            â”‚
â”‚                                                             â”‚
â”‚  AGENT LAYER (STATELESS):                                   â”‚
â”‚  â€¢ Multiple agents per data source (active-active)         â”‚
â”‚  â€¢ Automatic failover (< 5 seconds)                         â”‚
â”‚  â€¢ Local buffering (handles network outages)                â”‚

Color Palette:
Background: Dark navy/charcoal (consistent)

 - X marks: Red (âŒ)

 - Expanso box: Green highlight (winner)
 - Competitor boxes: Gray
 - Savings numbers: Bright green
 - Cost increases: Red
- **Positioning Map**:
 - Expanso: Gold star (â­) with bright highlight
 - Competitors: Standard markers

---

## **Why This Slide Works:**

### âœ… **Objective Comparison**
Shows competitors' strengths (builds credibility) while highlighting Expanso advantages

### âœ… **Multiple Perspectives**
Feature matrix, TCO analysis, positioning map, customer quotes = comprehensive view

### âœ… **Quantified Differences**
Specific savings numbers (50-70% vs. 35%) make differences concrete

### âœ… **Addresses "Why Not Them?"**
Proactively handles competitive objections with clear positioning

### âœ… **Complementary Positioning**
Shows when to use competitors WITH Expanso (partnership, not just competition)

### âœ… **Win/Loss Analysis**
Honest about when competitors might fit better (builds trust)

---

## **When to Use This Slide:**

### **Use During Presentation If:**
- Competitors already mentioned by prospect
- Competitive evaluation in progress
- RFP/vendor comparison process
- Champion needs ammunition vs. other vendors

### **Use as Backup If:**
- Early-stage discussion (don't introduce competitors)
- Executive audience (focus on value, not competition)
- No competitive threat identified

### **Always Have Ready For:**
- "How do you compare to [competitor]?" questions
- Competitive shoot-outs
- Final vendor selection
- Champion enablement

---

## **Presentation Script (When Delivering This Slide):**

### **Opening:**
> "You're probably evaluating other solutions, so let me be transparent about how we compare to the main alternatives you'll see."

### **Cribl Comparison:**
> "**[Point to Cribl column]** Cribl is a strong solution for observability pipelines. They do a great job optimizing SIEM costsâ€”typically 35% savings on Splunk or Datadog.

> **[Point to Expanso column]** Where Expanso is different: We handle ALL your enterprise data, not just observability. We optimize Snowflake, Databricks, AND your SIEM platforms. And we deliver 50-70% savings across your entire data estate, not just one category.

> The buyer is different too. Cribl typically sells to DevOps and SRE teams. We sell to Data Platform Engineering and FinOpsâ€”teams responsible for the entire data budget."

### **Fivetran Comparison:**
> "**[Point to Fivetran column]** Fivetran and Airbyte are excellent data integration tools. They have 500+ connectors and make it easy to replicate SaaS data into your warehouse.

> **[Point to Expanso column]** But here's the key difference: They move ALL your data, which is why your Snowflake bill keeps growing. We filter 50-70% of unnecessary data BEFORE it moves.

> **[Pause]** And here's what's interesting: Many of our customers use BOTH. They use Expanso upstream for optimization and Fivetran for SaaS connector breadth. They're complementary."

### **Monte Carlo Comparison:**
> "**[Point to Monte Carlo column]** Monte Carlo is the leader in data observability. They're excellent at detecting data quality issues in your warehouse.

> **[Point to Expanso column]** The fundamental difference: They detect problems downstream. We prevent problems upstream. They monitor data quality after data arrives. We filter bad data before it moves.

> And critically: They add cost to your stack. We reduce it by 50-70%."

### **TCO Analysis:**
> "**[Point to TCO comparison]** Let me show you the math over 3 years.

> With Cribl, you save about $4.6 millionâ€”but only on observability costs. Your analytics costs keep growing.

> With Fivetran, you actually ADD $900K to your total spend. They provide value through automation, but they don't reduce platform costs.

> With Expanso, you save $17.25 million over 3 yearsâ€”because we optimize ALL your platforms simultaneously.

> **[Point to Expanso box]** That's 3.7x better ROI than Cribl, and we're the only solution that dramatically reduces your total data spend."

### **Unique Differentiators:**
> "**[Point to unique differentiators]** So what does only Expanso do?

> We're the only platform that handles observability AND analytics AND IoT data in one solution.

> We're the only solution that reduces platform costs by 50-70%.

> We're the only platform that prevents problems upstream instead of detecting them downstream.

> And we're the only solution with predictable per-node pricingâ€”no consumption surprises."

### **Closing:**
> "Look, all of these vendors have their place. Cribl is great for observability-only use cases. Fivetran is excellent for SaaS connector breadth. Monte Carlo is strong for warehouse monitoring.

> But if you want to dramatically reduce your data platform costs across ALL your platformsâ€”Snowflake, Databricks, Splunk, Datadogâ€”while improving performance and automating compliance, Expanso is the only solution that delivers that."

---

## **Objection Handling Built Into This Slide:**

### **Objection 1: "We're already using [competitor]"**
**Answer Built In**: TCO comparison shows switching saves millions over 3 years

### **Objection 2: "Why not just use Cribl?"**
**Answer Built In**: Cribl only handles observability (35% savings), Expanso handles all data (50-70% savings)

### **Objection 3: "Can't we use Fivetran for this?"**
**Answer Built In**: Fivetran replicates, doesn't optimize. Use both together.

### **Objection 4: "What about Monte Carlo?"**
**Answer Built In**: Monte Carlo detects (and adds cost), Expanso prevents (and reduces cost)

### **Objection 5: "These tools seem complementary, not competitive"**
**Answer Built In**: Exactlyâ€”many customers use Expanso WITH these tools for best results

- Objection handling scripts
- Win/loss stories

### **2. TCO Calculator**
- Customizable for each prospect
- Compare Expanso vs. competitors
- 3-year financial analysis

### **3. Customer References**
- "Why we chose Expanso over [competitor]" stories
- Head-to-head evaluation case studies
- ROI comparisons

### **4. Analyst Reports**
- Gartner/Forrester positioning
- Market landscape analysis
- Category definitions

---

## **Common Questions This Slide Answers:**

### **Q: "How do you compare to Cribl?"**
**A**: Cribl = observability only, 35% savings. Expanso = all data, 50-70% savings

### **Q: "Why not just use Fivetran?"**
**A**: Fivetran moves data, doesn't reduce costs. Use both together.

### **Q: "What about Monte Carlo for data quality?"**
**A**: Monte Carlo detects downstream, we prevent upstream. Complementary.

### **Q: "Who are your main competitors?"**
**A**: Depends on use caseâ€”Cribl (observability), Fivetran (integration), Monte Carlo (quality)

### **Q: "Why should we choose you over them?"**
**A**: Only solution that reduces costs 50-70% across ALL platforms

### **Q: "Can we use you together with [competitor]?"**
**A**: Yes! Many customers use Expanso + Fivetran, or Expanso + dbt

When to Use This Slide:
Use During Presentation If:
Customer asks "What's on your roadmap?"

Always Have Ready For:

Product evaluation committees
Innovation-focused buyers

Objection Handling Built Into This Slide:
Objection 1: "Is this product mature enough?"
Answer Built In: Current capabilities section shows production-ready platform

Objection 2: "Will you have the features we need?"
Answer Built In: Customer-driven development + roadmap input

Objection 4: "What if our requirements change?"
Answer Built In: Quarterly roadmap reviews, customer advisory board

Objection 5: "Will you keep innovating?"
Answer Built In: Clear roadmap, strategic themes, research partnerships

"What If" Scenarios:

â”Œâ”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â” â”‚ COMMON "WHAT IF" SCENARIOS: â”‚ â”‚ â”‚ â”‚ Q: What if we filter the wrong data and lose insights? â”‚ â”‚ A: We use intelligent tiering, not deletion. Low-value â”‚ â”‚ data goes to S3 (still queryable, just cheaper). Plus: â”‚ â”‚ we help identify filtering opportunities during â”‚ â”‚ assessment. Start conservative, optimize over time. â”‚ â”‚ â”‚ â”‚ Q: What if our requirements change after deployment? â”‚ â”‚ A: Policies are easy to update (declarative YAML/JSON). â”‚ â”‚ Changes deploy in minutes. When to Use This Slide:
Use During Presentation If:
Customer asks "Tell me about your company"

Presentation Script (When Delivering This Slide):
Opening:
"Let me tell you a bit about who we are and why we built Expanso."

Mission:
"[Point to mission] Our mission is simple: eliminate the data tax that enterprises pay for unnecessary data processing. We saw this problem firsthand at Google, AWS, and Microsoftâ€”enterprises wasting billions moving data they never use."

Leadership Team:
"[Point to founders] We're not a typical startup. Our founding team comes from Google, AWS, and Microsoftâ€”we've built the very systems that enterprises rely on today.

David led Kubernetes and GKE at Google and co-founded Kubeflow. Walid architected AWS CloudWatch and Kinesis. Tony scaled operations at McKinsey and Microsoft.

We've operated data infrastructure at petabyte scale. We've lived the pain our customers feel."

Traction:
"[Point to growth metrics] Since founding in 2021, we've grown to 50+ enterprise customers including Fortune 500 companies and the U.S. Government. We've delivered over $100 million in customer value with a 95% retention rate.

More importantly: 100% of our customers achieve their target savings. Zero data loss incidents across all deployments. These aren't marketing claimsâ€”this is our track record."

Financial Stability:
"[Point to funding] We're backed by General Catalystâ€”the same tier-one VC that backed Stripe, Datadog, and Airbnb. We have 3+ years of runway, 200% year-over-year growth, and profitable unit economics.

You're not betting on a startup that might disappear. We're here for the long term."

Why It Matters:
"[Point to why customers trust us] When you choose Expanso, you're not just buying software. You're partnering with a team that's been in your shoes, a company that's financially stable, and a platform that's proven at Fortune 500 scale.

We're invested in your successâ€”literally. Your success is our success."

## **Deck Usage Guide:**

### **30-Minute Standard Presentation:**
- Use Slides 1-9 (core deck)
- Problem/Solution: 15 min
- Proof: 8 min
- Process & CTA: 7 min

### **15-Minute Executive Summary:**
- Use Slides 1, 2, 4, 6, 7, 9
- Skip detailed process
- Focus on problem, solution, proof, CTA

### **45-60 Minute Deep-Dive:**
- Use Slides 1-12 (core + technical)
- Core presentation: 25 min
- Enterprise readiness: 5 min
- Pricing: 5 min
- Technical architecture: 10 min
- Q&A: 15 min

### **Board/Executive Presentation:**
- Use Slides 1, 2, 6, 7, 10, 11, 17
- Focus on business value, proof, and credibility
- Skip technical details
